All rights reserved.\nHome\nRecipes\nPrev Recipe\nNext Recipe\nWATCH\nWATCH\nLoading Video...\nSee more\n(12)\nCaprese Chicken Penne Alfredo\nRecipe courtesy of Food Network Kitchen\nRecipe courtesy of Food Network Kitchen\nWatch how to make this recipe.\nCaprese Chicken Penne Alfredo\nGetting reviews...\nCreamy Alfredo pasta meets the freshness of a caprese salad in this one-skillet dinner.\nSave Recipe\nLevel:\nEasy\nTotal:\n1 hr\n(includes cooling time)\nActive:\n30 min\nYield:\n6 servings\nShare This Recipe\nPinterest\nFacebook\nTwitter\nEmail\nLevel:\nEasy\nTotal:\n1 hr\n(includes cooling time)\nActive:\n30 min\nYield:\n6 servings\nIngredients\n1 pound penne pasta\n8 tablespoons (1 stick) unsalted butter\n2 cloves garlic, finely grated\n3 cups heavy cream\n2 cups finely grated Parmesan\n2 cups chopped cooked white meat chicken (from 1 rotisserie chicken)\nKosher salt and freshly ground black pepper\n2 large red heirloom beefsteak tomatoes, sliced 1/4 inch thick\n1 pound fresh salted mozzarella, sliced 1/4 inch thick\n2 tablespoons extra-virgin olive oil\n1/2 cup torn fresh basil leaves\nDirections\nWATCH\nWatch how to make this recipe.\nPosition an oven rack in the center of the oven and preheat to 350 degrees F.\nCook the pasta to al dente according to the package directions. (Reserve some pasta water to add back in case the dish needs moisture.)\nMelt 2 tablespoons butter in a large skillet over medium-high heat and add the garlic. Cook, stirring occasionally, until very fragrant but not browned, about 1 minute. Add the cream and Parmesan and cook, stirring frequently until the mixture begins to boil, about 5 minutes. Add the chicken and cooked pasta and carefully toss to completely coat, then continue to cook until the mixture is smooth and thick, about 3 minutes. Season with salt and pepper and add the remaining 6 tablespoons butter. Carefully stir until the butter is completely melted and the sauce is glossy and creamy; remove from the heat.\u00a0\nAlternating 1 slice of tomato and 1 slice of mozzarella, shingle around the outer edge of the skillet creating a ring that covers the pasta. Repeat with the remaining tomato and mozzarella forming smaller concentric rings until the pasta is completely covered. Drizzle with the olive oil, sprinkle with some salt and bake until the mozzarella is beginning to melt but the slices still hold their shape and are still white, about 20 minutes. Let cool 10 minutes, then top with the basil and serve.\nCopyright 2018 Television Food Network, G.P. Alfredo-style Creamy Pesto Shrimp Alfredo is a winner with the whole family. Serve over zucchini noodles or cauliflower rice (OR pasta if you\u2019re not watching your carb intake)! The sauce is EVERYTHING.\nHow To Make Shrimp Alfredo\nSome Alfredo sauce recipes usually start with a roux, and some are based on butter/heavy cream. For the sake of keeping this recipe low carb and delicious, I went the butter/cream option, mixed with a homemade basil pesto and parmesan cheese. We added in blistered grape tomatoes to add even more flavour to the sauce, but you can leave them out if you wish!\nThis recipe is so easy it has only three steps to it:\nCook shrimp\nAdd sauce ingredients\nThicken\nWith the right quantity of each ingredient, you end up with a beautiful silky creamy pesto sauce perfect for serving over anything, really.\nLow carb Alfredo\nFor the low carb option, serve over zucchini noodles, cauliflower rice, or any steamed veggies you have on hand. You could also use Konjac noodles!\nPasta Alfredo\nPasta of choice is linguine and fettuccini. You can also serve with penne, spaghetti, or any other pasta you like.\nHow do you make shrimp Alfredo pasta?\nAdd 2 cups cooked pasta along with 1/4 cup of reserved pasta water into the sauce. Gently mix the sauce through until combined. Add in the shrimp and serve immediately.\nWhat can I use instead of heavy cream for Alfredo sauce?\nThe recipe includes half and half, which is\u00a0an American product made from equal parts light cream and milk. Substitute with half light cream and half 2% milk (or full fat if not worried about calories and fat counts). Alternatively, use all light cream or thickened cream.\nLove Creamy Shrimp? Try These!\nCreamy Shrimp Piccata\nCreamy Tuscan Shrimp\nCreamy Lemon Parmesan Shrimp\nCreamy Pesto Shrimp Alfredo\nCreamy Pesto Shrimp Alfredo with parmesan cheese and blistered tomatoes is the shrimp recipe of your dreams! Ready in less than 10 minutes, gluten free AND low carb! Alfredo-style Creamy Pesto Shrimp Alfredo is a winner with the whole family. Serve over zucchini noodles or cauliflower rice (OR pasta if you're not watching your carb intake)! The sauce is EVERYTHING.\nPRINT\nSAVE\ngo to your favorites\nPrep: 5\nmins\nCook: 10\nmins\nTotal: 15\nmins\nServes: 4\npeople\nIngredients\n2\ntablespoons\nunsalted butter\n1\npound\n(500 g) jumbo shrimp (or prawns),\ntails on or off\n4-5\ncloves\ngarlic,\nminced\n4\nounces\n(120g) grape tomatoes\n1/2\ncup\nbasil pesto\n1\ncup\nhalf and half or heavy cream*\nSEE NOTES\n1/2\ncup\nfresh grated Parmesan cheese,\ndivided\nSalt and pepper,\nto taste\n1\ntablespoon\nfresh parsley or basil,\nchopped\nInstructions\nHeat butter in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Add the shrimp and tomatoes, and season with salt and pepper to taste. Cook for 2 minutes, then add the garlic and cook for a further minute until shrimp starts to change colour and garlic is fragrant.\nReduce heat to low-medium heat. Add pesto, half & half (or heavy cream) and half of the parmesan cheese. Mix and scrape any bits off of the bottom of the pan.\nGently simmer for a further minute or two until shrimp is cooked, the sauce thickens slightly and the cheese has melted through. Sprinkle with parsley or basil and remaining parmesan cheese.\nServe immediately over pasta, rice, steamed veg, zucchini noodles or cauliflower rice.\nNotes\nHalf and half is an American product, made from equal parts light cream and milk. Substitute with half light cream and half 2% milk (or full fat if not worried about calories and fat counts). Alternatively, use all light cream or heavy cream.\nIf serving with pasta: add 2 cups cooked pasta along with 1/4 cup of reserved pasta water into the sauce. Gently mix the sauce through until combined. Add in the shrimp and serve immediately.\nNutrition\nCalories: 373 kcal | Carbohydrates: 7 g | Protein: 23 g | Fat: 22 g | Saturated Fat: 8 g | Cholesterol: 178 mg | Sodium: 150 mg | Potassium: 186 mg | Sugar: 1 g | Vitamin A: 1470 IU | Vitamin C: 6.7 mg | Calcium: 322 mg | Iron: 0.7 mg\nFiled Under: Dinner\nTagged With: alfredo , dinner , gluten free , low carb , pesto , shrimp\nSubscribe to Cafe Delites FOR FREE and Receive Recipes Straight Into Your Inbox!\nE-Mail Address\nPrevious Post: \u00ab 18 Best Salad Recipes\nNext Post: Potato Salad with Bacon & Dill Pickles \u00bb\nReader Interactions\nComments\nJoEllen\nsays\nApril 1, 2020 at\nThird time making this today! All Rights Reserved\n"], "_version_": 1665285015501537280, "score": 8.793887}, {"tstamp": ["2020-04-28T14:39:56.008Z"], "digest": ["7f54dfe662477d2739b22fd483e17017"], "host": ["jessicainthekitchen.com"], "boost": [0.3873124], "id": "https://jessicainthekitchen.com/vegan-garlic-alfredo-pasta/comment-page-1/", "title": ["Vegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta - Jessica In The Kitchen"], "url": ["https://jessicainthekitchen.com/vegan-garlic-alfredo-pasta/comment-page-1/"], "content": ["Vegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta - Jessica In The Kitchen\nHome\nAbout\nBuy our Ebook\nIt\u2019s That Easy Affiliates\nSubscribe\nRecipes\nGuides\nShop\nKitchen Essentials\nPantry Staples\nCookbooks\nNatural Beauty\nPhotography\nHome\nAbout\nRecipes\nGuides\nShop\nKitchen Essentials\nPantry Staples\nCookbooks\nNatural Beauty\nPhotography\nEBOOK\nSubscribe\nSearch\nSubmit\nVegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta\nRecipes | April 2, 2018\nThis Vegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta is such a creamy and cheesy weeknight dinner! It\u2019s absolutely decadent, made with a cashew cream sauce, and the sauce is made easily in your blender!\nWhere do I start? You\u2019re going to absolutely love and want to devour this Vegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta. I\u2019m talking cheesy, creamy, absolutely indulgent in taste kind of pasta dinner. The kind of dinner that totally hits the spot, and makes you want to curl up on a Friday night. Without the heavy feeling, of course. All my pasta cravings are hereby conquered.\nFirst things first \u2013 I haven\u2019t been a big pasta fanatic. LET me be clear. When a pasta dish is done well \u2013 I am all for that. If you\u2019re a vegetarian or a vegan though, you know that\u00a0 lots of pasta dishes just are\u00a0 not done correctly. Kind of a leftover, oh yeah whoops, kind of scenario, and it can drive you to never want to have pasta again.\nWHAT a terrible nightmarish scenario. Fortunately, after making this Vegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta, I now know I have the best pasta dish sitting and waiting at home on me! You\u2019re going to want to grab some cashews right now so that you can make this for dinner, friends.\nLet\u2019s talk key ingredients. That roasted garlic is a\u00a0 must . I mean, it deepens the flavour of the entire sauce, and really brings it to another level. You\u2019re going to have to wait for your cashews to soak anyway, so you might as well make it. I guarantee it\u2019ll change all of your dishes.\nSpeaking of which, cashews. OMG. Adding soaked cashews to this sauce makes it so creamy and gives it that traditional white colour. No, the sauce won\u2019t taste like cashews, thanks to the addition of another ingredient: lemon or lime juice. This acid helps to neutralise the cashew flavour so all you taste is the cheesiness.\nThe nutritional yeast and the vegan parmesan cheese! I speak all about nutritional yeast here , and I made a vegan parmesan cheese for you here. You can also buy your vegan parm though, so it\u2019s totally up to you. That extra bit of tanginess really ups the sauce, and you can add eons of it on top too. The nutritional yeast in the Alfredo sauce gives it that cheesy flavour, that will have you taste testing the heck out of this sauce.\nAlmond milk and pasta water! Don\u2019t use regular water! Pasta water already has some saltiness, some starch, and is a perfectly seasoned form of water in this sauce. The almond milk of course adds more creaminess.\nBasically what I\u2019m saying is, friends, every ingredient is key here. Including the cooked down onions (adding a nice flavour + umami). What you get is a beautiful vegan Alfredo sauce recipe made in your blender that you can pour back on your pasta and then dig in. The kind of sauce you\u2019ll probably want to put on anything, but will definitely slather all over your pasta.\nThat\u2019s it! Your pasta dreams have come true! Dive in friends, and enjoy!\n\u00a0\nVegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta\nby: Jessica in the Kitchen\nPrep Time 1\nminute\nCook Time 15\nminutes\nTotal Time 16\nminutes\nCourse Dinner, Lunch\nKeyword Dairy Free, Egg Free, Nut Free, Soy Free, vegan, Vegetarian\nPrint\nShare\nFacebook\nTwitter\nGoogle+\nPinterest\nYummly\nTumblr\nEmail\n5 from 3 votes\nIngredients\nPasta\n12\nounces\nany pasta\nI used fettuccine\nchopped parsley\nfor garnish\nVegan Alfredo Sauce\n2\nteaspoons\nvegan butter or olive oil\n1/2\nred onion\nchopped\n1\ncup\ncashews\nsoaked overnight, or in hot water for one hour\n1/4\ncup\npasta water\n1 \u00bd\ncups\nunsweetened almond milk\n4\ncloves\nroasted garlic*\n2\ntablespoons\nnutritional yeast\n\u00bd\nteaspoon\nsea salt\n2\ntablespoons\nvegan parmesan cheese + extra for topping\n1\ntablespoon\nlime juice\nInstructions\nInstructions\nCook pasta according to package directions in a well salted pot of water. Reserve \u00bc cup of the pasta water.\nWhile the pasta is boiling/you're waiting for the water to boil, in a pan over medium high heat, heat the vegan butter or olive oil. Add the onion, stir and let cook until translucent, about 5 minutes.\nRemove the onions from the pan and add it to a blender. Add the rinsed off soaked cashews (without the water), the pasta water, the almond milk, the roasted garlic, the nutritional yeast, the sea salt the vegan parmesan cheese and the lime juice. Blend it all together until completely creamy. If you have a high powered blender this will happen quickly, about 1 minute, if not, just keep blending until completely smooth and creamy. Taste and add more salt or vegan parmesan cheese if necessary.\nWhen the pasta is finished boiling, drain and pour back into the pan you had used earlier or even into a Tupperware container if you want. Pour the Alfredo sauce over and stir to combine completely.\nWhen serving, top with parsley to garnish and more vegan parmesan cheese. Enjoy!\nVideo\nNOTES\n*YES roasted garlic takes about 40 minutes, but you\u2019ll need to wait for your cashews to soak for an hour at least anyway! Cut a bit of the tops off of a whole head of garlic, put it in foil, drizzle olive oil on it, wrap the foil around it and cook it at 450 degrees F for 45 minutes in your oven until the cloves are soft and velvety! Allow it to cool, then push the cloves out.\n\u00a0\nYou can reheat this! Just reheat it in a stove top over medium high heat with a bit more almond milk to thin it out again until hot.\nPrep time doesn\u2019t include soaking the cashews overnight.\nby Jessica\n_-jbxMmYlqE\nShare This Post\nPost navigation\n\u2039\u2039 Older Posts\nNewer Posts \u203a\u203a\nYou Might Also Like\n10 Favourite Vegan Pumpkin Recipes to Celebrate Fall\nRead More\nVegan Arancini \u2013 Fried Rice Balls (Air Fryer Option!)\nRead More\nBanana Berry Beet Smoothie Bowl\nRead More\nleave a comment Cancel reply\nRecipe Rating\n40 comments\nComment navigation\nNewer Comments\nAlbert Bevia\nsays:\nI have always loved alfredo sauce but haven\u00b4t had it in a long time..it makes me feel to heavy and bloated, this vegan version sound like my answer to enjoying this sauce again, and so true, the roasted garlic does give a huge flavor\u2026thanks for the creative recipe \ud83d\ude42\nApril 4, 2018\nReply\nGavin | Jessica in the Kitchen\nsays:\nThanks so much Albert! I make it with shrimp for him for his birthday every year. GREAT for company because it is so easy and yet taste wonderful! I cook this in the microwave, but I'm sure you could do it on the stove too. Times are what work in my microwave. Please use your own good judgment on times to use in your microwave. (In my quest to eat healthier, I now make it with light butter, light cream and reduced fat Parmesan cheese. It still tastes wonderful, but there isn't any guilt!) PLEASE NOTE! This is an &quot;authentic&quot; Alfredo sauce recipe! Real Alfredo sauce *only* contains butter, cream, Parmesan cheese and pepper. It will be thin and there is no garlic in it! If you want a thicker sauce or one with garlic like modern restaurants serve, please look elsewhere! Recipe #52892 and Recipe #8596 are two good places to start.\n205\nPeople talking\nJoin In Now\nJoin the conversation!\nREADY IN:\n15mins\nSERVES:\n4\nUNITS:\nUS\nINGREDIENTS\nNutrition\n1 \u2044 4\nlb sweet butter (1/2 cup, light butter works fine!)\n1\ncup heavy cream or 1 cup light cream\n3 \u2044 4\ncup parmesan cheese , freshly grated\nsalt\n1 \u2044 4\nteaspoon pepper , freshly ground\nNUTRITION INFO\nServing Size: 1 (107) g\nServings Per Recipe: 4\nAMT. You\u2019ll be blown away how good this One Pot Alfredo Pasta is \u2013 the pasta is evenly cooked, the sauce is silky and creamy, not gluggy and thick. This is a game changer!!\nI\u2019m going to be honest with you, I\u2019ve had some bad experiences with one pot pastas.\u00a0When the one-pot pasta phenomenon started, thanks to Martha Stewart (though many Italians have since pointed out that they\u2019ve been doing it for\u00a0 years , it is just that Martha Stewart\u00a0made it popular and more widely known!), I was really cynical. Orzo, yes, it works great cooked in one pot with the sauce. Even macaroni and other short pasta.\u00a0But long pasta?\u00a0Then I tried Martha\u2019s original recipe and was lulled into a false sense of confidence and jumped right on board the one-pot pasta train.\nONE POT ALFREDO PASTA\nLike \u00a0this recipe? Pin it to your DINNER pinboard!\nFollow Real Housemoms on Pinterest\nBut then, disaster struck. Enticed by pretty photos, I tried a one pot creamy spaghetti. It was, to be frank (and I will never ever tell where I got the recipe from), bordering on inedible. And I like to think I have a cast iron stomach.\u00a0The pasta was unevenly cooked, the sauce was hideously gluggy, almost gluey.\u00a0It was an absolute disaster. One of the worst\u00a0things to come out of my kitchen in years.\nMost people would walk away and put it down to a bad recipe. Me? I was fuelled with a challenge. I was determined to come up with a way to make a creamy pasta in one pot.\u00a0It took a few goes but actually wasn\u2019t as hard as I expected. My thinking was that it\u2019s fat in the cream + the starch in the pasta that thickens the sauce. So all I do is add the cream right at the end. If you add it at the beginning, that\u2019s when you end up with gluggy sauce.\u00a0Less than 15 minutes.\u00a0A creamy Alfredo pasta with a luscious silky sauce.\u00a0YES, it\u2019s possible. And it is so, SO good.\nWant more easy pasta recipes?\nPizza Pasta Bake\nOne-Pot Spinach and Artichoke Pasta\nTaco Mac N Cheese Pasta Bake\nOne Pan Chicken Stroganoff\nCreamy Greek Shrimp Pasta\nPasta Carbonara\nMore dinner recipes\u2026\nTool used to make this One Pot Alfredo Pasta recipe\nLarge Skillet :\u00a0This skillet is my go-to kitchen tool. It\u2019s large circumference and high sides make it perfect for cooking anything from one pan meals to soups and sauces.\nTongs :\u00a0A good pair of tongs is a kitchen essential. I like having a couple sizes \u2013 a longer set for grilling and a shorter set for stovetop cooking.\nOne Pot Alfredo Pasta\nYes, you CAN make a creamy alfredo pasta in ONE POT! You'll be blown away how good this One Pot Alfredo Pasta is!\nPrint Recipe\nRate Recipe\nPrep Time: 3\nminutes\nCook Time: 12\nminutes\nTotal Time: 15\nminutes\nCourse: Main Dish\nServings: 3\nCalories: 743 kcal\nAuthor: Nagi @RecipeTinEats\nIngredients\n2\ncups\nmilk\nany fat %\n1 1/2\ncups\nchicken broth\n3\ntbsp\nbutter\n1\nlarge garlic clove\nminced\n8\nounces\nfettuccine\n1/2\ncup\nheavy cream\n3/4\ncup\nfreshly grated parmesan\nplus more for garnish\nSalt & pepper\nto taste\nParsley\nfor garnish\nInstructions\nUse a skillet large enough to fit the pasta.\nPlace skillet on the stove over medium-high heat. Add milk, chicken broth, butter, and garlic. Bring to simmer then add pasta.\nMove pasta around every 30 seconds or so until it is softened (around 3 minutes) so it doesn't stick. Once the pasta is softened, reduce heat to medium and stir every couple of minutes.\nAfter another 6 minutes or so, the pasta should be almost cooked but there should still be liquid covering the base of the skillet. Add cream and parmesan and mix.\nSimmer, stirring occasionally, for ~2 minutes, until sauce is thickened and pasta is cooked. If you cook it too long and the sauce goes gluggy, add a splash of hot tap water, it will go back to silky with a few tosses.\nAdjust salt and pepper to taste and serve immediately, garnished with freshly grated parmesan and parsley!\nVideo\nNutrition\nCalories: 743 kcal | Carbohydrates: 64 g | Protein: 26 g | Fat: 42 g | Saturated Fat: 24 g | Cholesterol: 186 mg | Sodium: 1014 mg | Potassium: 554 mg | Fiber: 2 g | Sugar: 9 g | Vitamin A: 1465 IU | Vitamin C: 8.5 mg | Calcium: 524 mg | Iron: 1.9 mg\nTried this recipe? We may earn money from the links on this page.\nFrench Onion Fettuccine Alfredo\nBy Makinze Gore\nFeb 27, 2020\nFettuccine Alfredo meets French Onion Soup in this crazy pasta dish. It's creamy and cheesy and is as decadent as we dream. To top off the dish Gruy\u00e8re gets melted over baguette slices and really sends this dish to the next level. It's not for the faint of heart.\u00a0\nHave you made this yet? Let us know how it went in the comments below!\u00a0\nRead More +\nRead Less -\nAdvertisement - Continue Reading Below\nYields: 6 servings\nPrep Time: 1 day 0 hours 15 mins\nTotal Time: 1 hour 30 mins\nIngredients\n1 lb.\nfettuccine\n6 tbsp.\nbutter, divided\n2\nlarge yellow onions, thinly sliced\u00a0\n1/4 c.\nwhite wine\u00a0\n4\ncloves garlic, minced\n4 tbsp.\nall-purpose flour\u00a0\n2 c.\nheavy cream\n2 c.\nmilk\n1/2 c.\nfreshly grated Parmesan\u00a0\n1 tsp.\nfresh thyme leaves\nKosher salt\u00a0\nFreshly ground black pepper\u00a0\nPinch crushed red pepper flakes\n2 1/2 c.\nshredded Gruy\u00e8re, divided\n1\nbaguette, thinly sliced\u00a0\nDirections\nPreheat oven to 350\u00b0. In a large pot of boiling salted water, cook pasta according to package directions until al dente. Drain.\u00a0\nIn a large skillet over medium heat, melt 2 tablespoons butter. Add onions and cook, stirring often, until deep golden and caramelized, about 30 minutes. Add white wine and continue to cook until evaporated, 5 minutes more.\nIn a medium skillet over medium heat, melt remaining 4 tablespoons butter. Add garlic and cook until fragrant, 1 minute. Add flour and cook until golden, 1 minute more. Slowly whisk in cream and milk. Bring mixture to a simmer, then add Parmesan and thyme and simmer until thickened, 5 minutes. Season with salt, pepper, and red pepper flakes.\u00a0\nAdd pasta to sauce and toss to combine. Top with caramelized onions and 1 cup Gruy\u00e8re.\u00a0Bake until cheese is melty, 20 minutes.\u00a0\nHeat oven to broil. Top pasta dish with baguette slices and top with remaining 1 \u00bd cup Gruy\u00e8re. Broil until golden, 5 minutes.\nCharlie Gillette\nMakinze Gore\nAssociate Food Editor\nMakinze is the Associate Food Editor for Delish.com.\nAdvertisement - Continue Reading Below\nMore From\nInsanely Easy Weeknight Dinners\nChicken Fried Rice\nClassic Stuffed Peppers\nAdvertisement - Continue Reading Below\nBeef Taco Salad\nGarlic Butter Shrimp Pasta\n36 Dinners That Are Done In 25 Minutes Or Less\nEven Meat Eaters Will <3 These Black Bean Burgers\nLoaded Zucchini Skins\nBest-Ever Lamb Burger\nKung Pao Brussels Sprouts\nEasy Mexican Rice\nInsanely Easy Weeknight Dinners\nRecipes\nMeals & Cooking\nFrench Onion Pork Chops\nAvocado Alfredo Pasta\nSkinny Alfredo Makes Eating Healthy Enjoyable\nKeto Burger Stuffed Onions\nChicken Alfredo Pizza\nChicken Alfredo Stuffed Spaghetti Squash\nNewsletter\nAbout Us\nPress Room\nContact Us\nBestProducts\nCommunity Guidelines\nAdvertise With Us\nA Part of Hearst Digital Media\nDelish participates in various affiliate marketing programs, which means we may get paid commissions on editorially chosen products purchased through our links to retailer sites.\n\u00a92020 Hearst Magazine Media, Inc. Who, me? Noooo, never. Okay, maybe. As the countdown to my move out of state begins and everything seems to be going haywire, I find myself needing a little comfort food. My usual go-to comfort food is pasta with butter, Parmesan, and salt and pepper, but today I decided to go a little further and make this creamy yet lightER Spinach Alfredo Pasta.\nGoes well with:\nHomemade Garlic Bread\nLighter Spinach Alfredo Pasta\nWhat is in Alfredo Sauce?\nSo, to be honest, this is not really an alfredo sauce (I actually wanted to call it \u201cfaux-fredo), but sometimes recipes names are a bit figurative. Real alfredo has like, a stick of butter, a pile of Parmesan, and sometimes (especially if you\u2019re in America) a whoooole lot of heavy cream.\nI swapped the heavy cream for whole milk, reduced the butter by a lot , and used a little cream cheese to help thicken and stabilize the sauce. So, it\u2019s no longer technically an alfredo, but hey, it\u2019s close enough for me to pretend and feel like I\u2019m eating something super indulgent.\nDoes Spinach Alfredo Pasta Reheat Well?\nThis Lighter Spinach Alfredo Pasta is definitely better when fresh (although I would NEVER turn down leftovers of this), so if you\u2019re cooking for one or two consider cutting the recipe in half. Luckily, this one is super easy to scale up or down. Just change the number of servings in the \u201cservings\u201d box on the recipe card below and the ingredients will auto-adjust.\n\u00a0\nPrint Recipe\n4.48 from 21 votes\nLighter Spinach Alfredo Pasta\nCreamy and rich, yet never heavy, this Lighter Spinach Alfredo Pasta is an easy and satisfying comfort food.\u00a0\nTotal Cost: $5.92 recipe / $1.48 serving\nPrep Time: 5\nmins\nCook Time: 20\nmins\nTotal Time: 25\nmins\nServings: 4\nIngredients\n12\noz\npenne pasta\n($0.74)\n2\nTbsp\nbutter\n($0.27)\n2\ncloves\ngarlic, minced\n($0.16)\n2\ncups\nwhole milk\n($0.62)\n6\noz.\ncream cheese\n($1.50)\n3/4\ncup\ngrated Parmesan\n($1.23)\n1/4\ntsp\nsalt\n($0.02)\nFreshly cracked pepper\n($0.05)\n4\ncups\nbaby spinach\n($1.33)\nUS Customary - Metric\nInstructions\nBring a large pot of water to a boil to cook the pasta. Once boiling, add the pasta and cook until al dente. Drain the pasta in a colander.\nWhile the pasta is cooking, prepare the sauce. Add the butter and minced garlic to a deep skillet or pot and saut\u00e9 over medium heat for 1-2 minutes, or just until the garlic is soft and fragrant, but not brown.\nTurn the heat down to medium-low. Add the milk to the skillet along with the cream cheese (cut into chunks). Heat the milk and cream cheese while whisking, until the cream cheese has fully melted into the milk.\nWhisk in the grated Parmesan cheese and continue to whisk as the sauce comes up to a gentle simmer. When it reaches a simmer, the sauce will thicken. Turn the heat down to low to keep the sauce warm. Season the sauce with 1/4 tsp salt and a generous amount of freshly cracked pepper.\nAdd the fresh spinach to the sauce and stir it in until it has wilted and become limp.\nFinally, add the cooked and drained pasta to the spinach alfredo sauce and stir to combine. Serve immediately.\nNutrition\nServing: 1 Serving \u30fb Calories: 663.73 kcal \u30fb Carbohydrates: 80.1 g \u30fb Protein: 24.43 g \u30fb Fat: 20.65 g \u30fb Sodium: 821.43 mg \u30fb Fiber: 3.4 g\nNutritional values are estimates only. See our full nutrition disclosure here .\nTried this recipe? Mention @budgetbytes or tag #budgetbytes on Instagram!\nThe equipment section above contains affiliate links to products we use and love!\nStep by Step Photos\nStart by cooking 12 oz. penne pasta according to the package directions (boil a large pot of water, add the pasta, and continue to boil until al dente). While the pasta is cooking, start the \u201calfredo\u201d sauce. Mince two cloves of garlic and add them to a deep skillet or pot with 2 Tbsp butter. Saut\u00e9 over medium heat for 1-2 minutes, or just until the garlic is soft and fragrant, but not brown.\nAdd 2 cups of whole milk to the skillet and turn the heat down to medium-low.\nAlso add 6 oz. cream cheese, cut into chunks. Heat and stir or whisk the milk and cheese until it is fully heated through and the cheese has melted into the milk. You\u2019ll want to use a whisk once the cheese begins to melt.\nWhisk 3/4 cup grated Parmesan into the milk sauce. Continue to whisk while the mixture heats, allowing it to come up to a gentle simmer. When it reaches a simmer, the sauce will thicken. Once the Parmesan has fully melted in and the sauce has thickened, turn the heat down to low to keep the sauce warm. Season the sauce with 1/4 tsp salt and a generous amount of freshly cracked pepper.\nNow it\u2019s time to add the spinach. I buy these huge bags of fresh spinach, which are the same amount as those large tubs you can buy, but it\u2019s only $3.99 (the large tubs are usually more like $5.99). Anyway, add about 4 cups of spinach to the hot alfredo sauce\u2026\nAnd stir it in until it has wilted and limp. This should only take a few minutes.\nFinally, add the cooked and drained penne pasta and stir until everything is combined and coated in the thick sauce.\nAnd that\u2019s it! Now you\u2019re ready to get your pasta on.\nSeriously though, this Lighter Spinach Alfredo Pasta is rich and creamy without being like, \u201cOMG I just ate a brick.\u201d\u00a0\nI\u2019m all about that cracked pepper. \ud83e\udd24\nRelated Posts\nCreamy Pesto Mac with Spinach\nOne Pot Creamy Sun Dried Tomato Pasta\nCreamy Tomato and Spinach Pasta\nBacon and Spinach Pasta with Parmesan\nposted on July 26, 2017 in Egg Free , Main Dish , Pasta Recipes , Quick , Recipe Archives , Sauce , Soy Free\n58 Comments \u00bb\n58 comments on \u201cLighter Spinach Alfredo Pasta\u201d\n\u00ab Older Comments\nLouise \u2014\n04.11.20 @ 4:05 pm\nReply\nI loved it\nMichele \u2014\n02.23.20 @ 6:26 pm\nReply\nYummy! Please read my disclosure policy .\nIf you\u2019ve wondered how to make Chicken Alfredo with less calories and loads of flavor, look no further. \u00a0This recipe cuts the calories by about 65% yet gets rave reviews every time!\nChicken Alfredo .. delish! \u00a0Seriously this is so good!\nDid you know when you order Chicken Alfredo at your average restaurant,\u00a0\u00a0you are ordering a whopping 1200 \u2013 1547 calories and up to 97 grams of fat! \u00a0CRAZY huh?\nThis recipe has just a fraction of the fat and\u00a0calories with all of the flavor\u00a0and only about\u00a0425 calories and 11 grams of fat. \u00a0Much better!\nAlfredo is an absolute favorite of both of my girls, I think they would eat it every single day if they could. \u00a0I decided it was time\u00a0figure out how to make Chicken Fettuccine\u00a0healthier for them and guess what\u2026 \u00a0the results were AMAZING! \u00a0Honestly, this recipe will knock your socks off\u00a0.. rich, creamy and oh so delicious!! \u00a0This has all of the flavor without all of the fat!\nI sometimes add in steamed broccoli, asparagus or mushrooms to get some extra veggies in. \u00a0You can also use whole wheat noodles or even zucchini noodles if you have a spiralizer .\nAs I learned at our local culinary school, nutmeg is an ingredient that is commonly added to white sauces. \u00a0You need just a small little pinch\u00a0to add\u00a0flavor to the sauce.\nThis recipe calls for 2 cups of cooked chicken. \u00a0You can either cook the chicken with a little bit of non-stick spray in a frying pan, use a store bought rotisserie chicken or (my favorite) grill it!\nREPIN this\u00a0Alfredo Recipe\n4.29 from 7 votes\nReview Recipe\nSKINNY CHICKEN FETTUCCINE ALFREDO\nPrep Time 15\nminutes\nCook Time 15\nminutes\nTotal Time 30\nminutes\nServings 8\nservings\nAuthor Holly Nilsson\nCourse Dinner\nCuisine American\nIf you\u2019ve wondered how to make Chicken Alfredo with less calories and loads of flavor, look no further. This recipe cuts the calories by about 65% yet gets rave reviews every time!\nPrint Pin\nIngredients\n2\nchicken breasts\ncooked and chopped\n1\ncup\ncold milk\n1\ntablespoon\nflour\n1\nteaspoon\nolive oil\n1\nclove\ngarlic\n3\ntablespoons\nlight cream cheese\nnot fat free\n\u00bd\ncup\nfresh parmesan cheese\nshredded\nsalt to taste\npinch\nnutmeg\n12\noz\nfresh fettuccine\nfresh parsley to taste\nInstructions\nOver medium heat, put olive oil and garlic in a pan. Cook about 1 minute.\nAdd flour to cold milk until dissolved and add to pan. Cook over medium heat while stirring constantly. Once thickened, turn heat off stir in cream cheese, salt & nutmeg until melted. Add parmesan and chicken.\nMeanwhile, cook pasta according to package directions. Toss pasta with sauce and top with parsley and additional cheese.\nNutrition Information\nCalories: 290 , Carbohydrates: 33 g , Protein: 21 g , Fat: 7 g , Saturated Fat: 2 g , Cholesterol: 82 mg , Sodium: 214 mg , Potassium: 372 mg , Fiber: 1 g , Sugar: 2 g , Vitamin A: 175 IU , Vitamin C: 0.8 mg , Calcium: 134 mg , Iron: 1.1 mg\nKeyword chicken alfredo\n\u00a9 SpendWithPennies.com. Cook the pasta according to the package directions. Drain and set aside.\nSlice the chicken into thin strips and season with salt and pepper. Heat the butter and oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Add the chicken strips and cook until deep golden brown on both sides and done in the middle. Remove the chicken from the skillet and add the minced garlic. Cook the garlic for 1 minute, then pour in the broth. Let it bubble up and reduce for 1 1/2 to 2 minutes.\nNext, add the half-and-half, cream and some salt and pepper. Add the Parmesan, whisking constantly until it's all combined. Allow the liquid to heat up and thicken for a few minutes. If it gets too thick, you may thin it with a little chicken broth.\nWhen the sauce looks good, remove it from the heat. Return the cooked chicken to the skillet along with the grape tomatoes, spinach and pasta. We\u2019ve got loads of flavour packed into this simple, hearty dish.\nFrom the number of pasta bakes and\u00a0 other pasta recipes on our site, I think you can guess how much we love pasta.\nI often make tomato-based pasta dishes, but today I felt like sharing a rich and creamy pasta bake . This one is definitely rich! Pasta smothered in a creamy sauce with a little garlic and a hint of white wine (optional) with parmesan, cheddar AND mozzarella! Not forgetting the shredded chicken (a great way to use up leftover chicken) and lots of lovely mushrooms.\nJust talking about it makes me want to eat it all over again.\nSo what exactly is alfredo sauce?\nIt\u2019s a very simple white sauce, usually made with butter , cream and parmesan . It\u2019s most commonly seen with the Italian classic Fettucine alfredo.\nI\u2019m going with a similar flavour profile here, but with some added extras (such as garlic and more cheese!) to make it even more delicious.\nWhat do we need to make this bake?\nThis recipe uses leftover cooked chicken from your Roast Chicken Dinner.\nMore recipes using cooked leftover chicken:\nTuscan Chicken Soup\nCreamy Chicken and Potato Bake\nRoast Chicken & Creamy Garlic Mushroom Burger\nChicken ala King\nGarlic Chicken Pasta with Kale\nHere are the simple steps:\nFull ingredient quantities and instructions are in the recipe card below.\nSoften a chopped onion in a large frying pan with a little oil. Then add in mushrooms, salt, pepper and garlic, and cook for a few minutes, until the mushrooms are tender.\nNext in goes the white wine that we bubble for a few minutes before adding in chicken stock, cream, shredded chicken and parmesan.\nHeat through, while stirring, until the parmesan melts , then add cooked drained pasta and stir again.\nTransfer to a large baking dish and sprinkle on parmesan, cheddar and mozzarella.\nThen bake in the oven for 20-25 minutes until the cheese is golden brown .\nMore pasta bakes:\nCheesy Chicken Pasta Bake With Bacon (this is a tomato-based one)\nCreamy Tuna Pasta Bake\nSmoky Meatball Pasta Bake from my friend Ciara\u2019s book\u00a0 My Fussy Eater (<\u2013 affiliate link)\nSausage Pasta Bake with Chorizo and Brie\nI need your help!\nWhat would you like to see in a pasta bake? I\u2019d love to make some more, but I want to make sure I get it just right for you guys. A veggie pasta bake,\u00a0 A meaty one, a fish pasta bake or something else? Please let me know in the comments below.\nThe video:\nWhats our video on YouTube to see exactly how to make this delicious Creamy Chicken Pasta Bake\nCreamy Chicken Alfredo Pasta Bake\nCreamy, cheesy and filling - this Chicken Alfredo Pasta Bake with mushrooms makes a fantastic comforting dinner.\n5 from 4 votes\nPrint\nRate\nPin The Recipe For Later\nPrep Time: 10\nmins\nCook Time: 40\nmins\nTotal Time: 50\nmins\nCourse: Dinner\nCuisine: American, Italian\nKeyword: Alfredo Pasta Bake, Alfredo Sauce, Comfort Food, pasta bake\nServings: 6\nAuthor: Nicky Corbishley\nIngredients\n14\noz\n(400g) dried pasta\n(I used fusilli)\n2\ntbsp\nolive oil\n1\nonion\npeeled and finely chopped\n1/2\nlb\n(230g) baby chestnut mushrooms\nsliced in half\n1/2\ntsp\nsalt\n1/2\ntsp\nblack pepper\n2\ncloves\ngarlic\nminced\n1/2\ncup\n(120ml) white wine\n1/2\ncup\n(120ml) chicken stock\n1\ncup\n(240ml) double (heavy) cream\n2\ncooked skinless chicken breasts\nroughly chopped or shredded\n1\ncup\n(100g) finely grated parmesan\n1/2\ncup\n(50g) strong cheddar\ngrated/shredded\n1/2\ncup\n(50g) mozzarella cheese\ngrated/shredded\n1\nsmall bunch of parsley\nroughly torn\nInstructions\nPreheat the oven to 190c/375f. Boil a large pan of water and cook the pasta for 1 minute less than recommended on the pack. Drain.\nWhilst the pasta is cooking, heat the oil on a medium heat, in a large frying pan. Add the onion and cook for 4-5 minutes, stirring occassionally, until the onion softens.\nAdd the mushrooms, salt, pepper and garlic, and cook for a further 3-4 minutes, stirring often, until the mushrooms are tender.\nAdd the white wine, turn up the heat to high and allow the wine to bubble for a few minutes until reduced by half, then turn the heat back down to medium.\nAdd the chicken stock, cream, shredded chicken and half of the parmesan and stir together until the cheese melts.\nBy now the pasta should be cooked. Add the drained pasta to the pan and stir together until the pasta is coated in the creamy sauce.\nTransfer the contents of the pan to a large baking dish. Sprinkle the remaining parmesan and the cheddar and mozzarella on top, then place in the oven for 20-25 minutes until the cheese is golden brown.\nRemove from the oven and sprinkle with parsley before serving.\nRecipe Video\nRecipe Notes\nWhat type of pasta to use:\nI use Fusilli for this, but you can use any larger-sized pasta you like - such as Spiralli (pasta spirals), Penne (tubes cut on the diagonal), Rigatoni (ribbed pasta tubes, square-cut on the ends) and Farfalle (pasta bows) all work particularly well, with no change in amounts or cooking times. You can also use Ziti - which is similar to Rigatoni, but a little smaller and not ribbed (unless you buy Ziti Rigati - which is ribbed). I was thinking of making this dish a baked alfredo ziti, but ziti pasta is very difficult to find in the UK.\nCan I make it ahead?\nYes! You can make ahead up to the point where you have sprinkled the cheese on, then cool, cover with foil and refrigerate for up to a day. Take out of the fridge for an hour before cooking it, to take the chill off the dish (otherwise you mind find you get a cold spot in the middle when baking it). Keep the foil on and heat in the oven at 190C/375F for about 10 minutes, then remove the foil and continue to heat for a further 15 minutes, until hot throughout. Note: the dish will be a little less saucy if you make it ahead, as the pasta will absorb more of the liquid. You can a few tablespoons of stock or hot water before heating the pasta to ensure it\u2019s still saucy if you like.\nWill it freeze?\nYes, once cooked: Cool quickly, cover and freeze. Defrost in the refrigerator overnight, then take out of the fridge for an hour before cooking it. Reheat in the oven (covered in foil) at 190C/375F for about 20-25 minutes until hot throughout. Add a few tablespoons of stock or hot water when reheating the pasta to ensure it\u2019s still saucy.\nNutritional information is per serving (this recipe contains 6 servings)\nNutritional Information\nNutrition Facts\nCreamy Chicken Alfredo Pasta Bake\nAmount Per Serving\nCalories 666\nCalories from Fat 288\n% Daily Value*\nFat 32g 49%\nSaturated Fat 17g 85%\nCholesterol 122mg 41%\nSodium 779mg 32%\nPotassium 531mg 15%\nCarbohydrates 56g 19%\nFiber 3g 12%\nSugar 4g 4%\nProtein 35g 70%\nVitamin A 908IU 18%\nVitamin C 2mg 2%\nCalcium 360mg 36%\nIron 2mg 11%\n* Percent Daily Values are based on a 2000 calorie diet.\nTried this recipe? Sprinkle with remaining cheese, the reserved walnuts and more parsley. All rights reserved.\nHome\nRecipes\nPrev Recipe\nNext Recipe\nCreamy Cauliflower Alfredo\nRecipe courtesy of Food Network Kitchen\nRecipe courtesy of Food Network Kitchen\nWatch how to make this recipe.\nCreamy Cauliflower Alfredo\nGetting reviews...\nThe key to a tasty fettuccine alfredo is a creamy sauce. By cooking and blending cauliflower to a smooth puree, you get the creamy mouthfeel of butter and cream without the high calories and fat.\nSave Recipe\nLevel:\nIntermediate\nTotal:\n1 hr\nPrep:\n25 min\nCook:\n35 min\nYield:\n4 servings\nNutrition Info\nNutritional Analysis\nPer Serving\nCalories\n324\nTotal Fat\n7 grams\nSaturated Fat\n3.5 grams\nCholesterol\n17 milligrams\nSodium\n326 milligrams\nCarbohydrates\n53 grams\nDietary Fiber\n10 grams\nProtein\n16 grams\nShare This Recipe\nPinterest\nFacebook\nTwitter\nEmail\nLevel:\nIntermediate\nTotal:\n1 hr\nPrep:\n25 min\nCook:\n35 min\nYield:\n4 servings\nNutrition Info\nNutritional Analysis\nPer Serving\nCalories\n324\nTotal Fat\n7 grams\nSaturated Fat\n3.5 grams\nCholesterol\n17 milligrams\nSodium\n326 milligrams\nCarbohydrates\n53 grams\nDietary Fiber\n10 grams\nProtein\n16 grams\nIngredients\n2 cups cauliflower florets, about 8-ounces\n1 cup low-sodium chicken broth\n8 ounces whole grain fettuccine pasta\n1 teaspoon extra-virgin olive oil\n2 cloves garlic, minced\n1/2 cup low-fat evaporated milk\nKosher salt and freshly ground pepper\n3/4 cup frozen petite peas, thawed, (4 ounces)\n1/4 cup grated Parmesan cheese\n1 tablespoon unsalted butter\n1 tablespoon chopped fresh parsley, plus extra for garnish\n1 1/2 teaspoons finely grated lemon zest\nDirections\n1. Put the cauliflower, broth, and 1 cup water in a small pot; bring to a boil over medium-high heat. Adjust the heat to maintain a simmer and cook until the cauliflower is very soft, 25 to 30 minutes. Remove from the heat and cool 5 minutes. Carefully puree cauliflower and all the liquid in a blender until very smooth; set aside.\n2. Meanwhile, bring a large pot of salted water to a boil and cook the pasta until al dente, 8 minutes. Drain well, reserving about 1 cup pasta cooking water.\n3. Heat the oil in a large skillet over medium heat. Add the garlic and cook until fragrant, about 30 seconds. Add the cauliflower puree and evaporated milk and bring to a simmer. Cook until slightly thickened, 5 minutes and season with salt and pepper. Stir in the peas until heated through, 2 minutes. Toss in the cooked pasta, Parmesan cheese and about 1/2 cup of pasta water until the noodles are coated but the sauce is still loose. Remove from the heat and toss in the butter, chopped parsley and lemon zest. (If the sauce seems thick, adjust the consistency with the remaining pasta water). Serve immediately sprinkled with chopped parsley.\nCopyright 2010 Television Food Network, G.P. All rights reserved.\nHome\nRecipes\nGuy Fieri\nPrev Recipe\nNext Recipe\nCajun Chicken Alfredo 2\nRecipe courtesy of Guy Fieri\nRecipe courtesy of Guy Fieri\nShow:\nThe Best Thing I Ever Made\nEpisode:\nThe Sure Thing\nCajun Chicken Alfredo 2\nGetting reviews...\nSave Recipe\nLevel:\nEasy\nTotal:\n45 min\nPrep:\n20 min\nCook:\n25 min\nYield:\n4 servings\nShare This Recipe\nPinterest\nFacebook\nTwitter\nEmail\nLevel:\nEasy\nTotal:\n45 min\nPrep:\n20 min\nCook:\n25 min\nYield:\n4 servings\nIngredients\nKosher salt\nFour 5-ounce boneless, skinless chicken breasts (about 1 1/4 pounds)\nBlackening Spice Rub, recipe follows\n2 tablespoons olive oil\n3 tablespoons minced garlic\n1/4 cup dry white wine\n3 cups heavy cream\n1 cup roughly chopped marinated sun-dried tomatoes\n1 pound fettuccine\n3/4 cup grated Parmesan\n1 teaspoon fine sea salt\n1 teaspoon freshly ground black pepper\n1/2 cup thinly sliced green onion, for garnish\nBlackening Spice Rub:\n1 tablespoon granulated garlic\n1 tablespoon freshly cracked black pepper\n1/2 tablespoon salt\n2 teaspoons ground cumin\n2 teaspoons granulated onion\n1 teaspoon cayenne pepper\n1 teaspoon Italian seasoning\n1 teaspoon paprika\n1/2 teaspoon chili powder\nDirections\nPreheat the oven to 350 degrees F. Bring a large pot of salted water to a boil. Heat a large cast-iron skillet over very high heat.\u00a0\nDredge the chicken breasts in the Blackening Spice Rub. Place in the cast-iron skillet. Blacken both sides of the chicken, 2 to 3 minutes per side.\u00a0\nTransfer the chicken to a baking sheet and place in the oven until the internal temperature of the chicken reaches 165 degrees F on an instant-read thermometer, about 10 minutes.\u00a0\nRemove from the oven and slice the chicken into strips on the bias.\u00a0\nIn a large skillet over medium heat, heat the olive oil. Add the garlic and lightly brown it, 2 to 3 minutes. Stir in the wine. Pour in the heavy cream, bring to a simmer and cook until the sauce is reduced by half. Add the sun-dried tomatoes and chicken slices.\u00a0\nMeanwhile, cook the fettuccine al dente, according to the package directions. Drain.\u00a0\nWhen the cream sauce is at the desired consistency, stir in 1/2 cup of the Parmesan, the sea salt, pepper and pasta.\u00a0\nTo serve, toss the pasta with the cream sauce and serve on large rimmed plates. Garnish with the green onions and the remaining 1/4 cup Parmesan.\nBlackening Spice Rub:\nCombine the garlic, black pepper, salt cumin, onion, cayenne pepper, Italian seasoning, paprika and chili powder in a small bowl. I like to use Frank's cayenne pepper sauce, but if you like things on the milder side, just use a little less. &mdash;Lauren Wyler, Dripping Springs, Texas\nBuffalo Chicken Alfredo Recipe photo by Taste of Home\nNext Recipe\nTest Kitchen Approved\nBe the first to review\nFeatured In\n30 Creative Quarantine Meals You Haven\u2019t Tried Yet\nRate\nComment\nSave\nPrint\nNext Recipe\nRate\nComment\nSave\nShare\nPrint\nTotal Time\nPrep/Total Time: 25 min.\nMakes\n4 servings\nRead Next\nThe Ultimate Age-Appropriate Chore Chart for Kids\nHow to Make a Quick and Simple Hand Sanitizer\n8 Tips for Setting Up a Productive Home Office\nIngredients\n1-1/4 cups chicken stock\n1 package (16 ounces) potato gnocchi\n2 cups shredded cooked chicken\n1 cup reduced-fat Alfredo sauce\n3 tablespoons Buffalo wing sauce\n1/3 cup crumbled blue cheese\n1/3 cup finely chopped celery with leaves\nView Recipe\nDirections\nPlace stock in a large skillet. We may earn money from the links on this page.\nShrimp Fettuccine Alfredo\nBy Lena Abraham\nOct 15, 2018\nFettuccine alfredo is one of life's greatest comfort foods. It's creamy, cheesy, carb-y, and super super flavorful. We especially love this version because the shrimp adds lots of extra flavor and some lean protein to boot! Make sure to avoid the common mistakes listed below and you'll master this dish in no time.\nOvercooking the pasta.\nNothing is worse than a bowl of mushy pasta. We're going for\u00a0 al dente in this recipe\u2014aka it should still have some bite. This can be especially tricky when you're adding cooked pasta back to a hot pan because it will actually get cooked a little bit more. We recommend tasting your pasta for doneness a 3 to 4 minutes before the box recommends. There should still be a bit of firmness in the center of your fettuccine. That means, given a little extra cooking time in the skillet you make the sauce in, it'll come out perfectly.\u00a0\nOvercooking the shrimp.\nNever underestimate how fast shrimp can cook. Depending on their size and the heat of your pan they could cook in literally one minute, so keep an eye on them!\u00a0As soon as they turn from gray and translucent to pink and opaque, they're good to go! Set them aside on a plate and continue with the sauce. Just don't ditch anything they've left behind in the pan!\u00a0Those juices (sorry) will help flavor your sauce and make it\u00a0 so\u00a0 much better.\nCurdling the sauce.\nOne of the secrets to making an extra creamy alfredo sauce is the addition of an egg yolk. In order to incorporating that yolk without cooking it, you need to make the sauce in a specific order. After you've added your flour, add your cold milk and cream\u00a0 first , so that when you drop your yolk in, it won't start cooking immediately. When you\u00a0 do\u00a0 drop your yolk in, whisk it in to the sauce immediately and you won't have any problems. If it still sounds risky to you, you can whisk together your heavy cream, milk, and yolk and pour it into your pan as a homogenous mixture.\nUsing cheap parm.\nThis creamy sauce is totally dependent on the cheese. Most of the pre-grated parmesan cheeses sold at the grocery store are mixed with preservatives in order to prevent caking and keep the pre-grated cheese dry. Unfortunately, this can lead to a less than favorable texture, and can make it more difficult for the cheese to melt. If you can, splurge for a real piece of Parmigiano Reggiano (or another hard cheese like Locatelli or Pecorino Romano). It'll make your alfredo sauce a bit more smooth and creamy.\u00a0\nRead More +\nRead Less -\nAdvertisement - Continue Reading Below\nYields: 4\nPrep Time: 0 hours 15 mins\nTotal Time: 0 hours 25 mins\nIngredients\n1 lb.\nfetuccine\n3 tbsp.\nbutter, divided\n1 lb.\nshrimp, peeled and deveined, tails removed\nkosher salt\nFreshly ground black pepper\n2\ncloves garlic, minced\n2 tbsp.\nall-purpose flour\n1 c.\nheavy cream\n1/2 c.\nwhole milk\n1\negg yolk\n1 c.\nfreshly grated Parmesan, plus more for garnish\n1 tbsp.\nChopped parsley, for garnish\nDirections\nCook fettuccine according to the instructions on box, reserving a cup of pasta water to thicken the sauce, if needed.\nIn a large skillet over medium heat, heat 1 tablespoon butter until melted. Add shrimp, season with salt and pepper and cook until pink and completely opaque, 2 to 3 minutes per side. Remove shrimp from skillet and set aside.\nInto the pan, add remaining 2 tablespoons butter and garlic. Cook until the garlic becomes fragrant, about 1 minute. Whisk in flour and cook until no longer raw, 2 minutes. Stir in heavy cream and milk, then whisk in egg yolk.\u00a0 Bring to a low simmer and whisk in parmesan. When cheese is melted and sauce has thickened slightly, add\u00a0cooked pasta and shrimp, tossing to combine. Season with salt and pepper.\nGarnish with more parmesan and parsley.\nEthan Calabrese\nDelish: Eat Like Every Day's the Weekend\nbarnesandnoble.com\n$20.85\nGET YOURS NOW\nLena Abraham\nFood Editor\nLena Abraham is the Food Editor at Delish, where she develops and styles recipes for video and photo, and also stays on top of current food trends.\nAdvertisement - Continue Reading Below\nMore From\nRecipes\n14 Game-Changing Iced Coffee Hacks\n79 Stupid-Easy Desserts That Only Look Impossible\nAdvertisement - Continue Reading Below\nChicken Fried Rice\nChurro Pull-Apart Muffins\n100+ Brilliant Ways to Top A Burger\nHomemade Rugelach\n\"Fried\" Ice Cream\nSpinach Artichoke Orzo\nTortilla Stromboli\nVegetarian Baked Ziti Is Cheesy Perfection\nRecipes\nMeals & Cooking\nBest Garlicky Shrimp Alfredo Bake\nEasy Chicken Alfredo Recipe\n20+ Super Healthy Shrimp Recipes\nHow to Cook Shrimp\nThe Best Ever Shrimp Scampi\nDelicious Shrimp Fried Rice Recipe\nNewsletter\nAbout Us\nPress Room\nContact Us\nBestProducts\nCommunity Guidelines\nAdvertise With Us\nA Part of Hearst Digital Media\nDelish participates in various affiliate marketing programs, which means we may get paid commissions on editorially chosen products purchased through our links to retailer sites.\n\u00a92020 Hearst Magazine Media, Inc. All Rights Reserved.\nPrivacy Notice\nYour California Privacy Rights\nInterest-Based Ads\nTerms of Use\nSite Map\nDo Not Sell My Info\n"], "_version_": 1665275985730207745, "score": 8.459258}, {"tstamp": ["2020-04-28T14:56:41.668Z"], "digest": ["2ae696cf73206bb7f9b262b34ad29bb8"], "host": ["www.foodnetwork.com"], "boost": [0.3873124], "id": "https://www.foodnetwork.com/recipes/valerie-bertinelli/chicken-and-broccoli-fettuccine-alfredo-with-homemade-fettuccine-3864846", "title": ["Chicken and Broccoli Fettuccine Alfredo with Homemade Fettuccine Recipe | Valerie Bertinelli | Food "], "url": ["https://www.foodnetwork.com/recipes/valerie-bertinelli/chicken-and-broccoli-fettuccine-alfredo-with-homemade-fettuccine-3864846"], "content": ["Chicken and Broccoli Fettuccine Alfredo with Homemade Fettuccine Recipe | Valerie Bertinelli | Food Network\nMagazine\nApp\nSaves\nArtboard (1)\nCreated with Sketch.\nFood Network Kitchen\nRecipes\nHealthy\nComfort Food\nShop\nShows\nChefs\nSchedule\nWatch Full Seasons\nRecipes\nShows\nChefs\nRestaurants\nVideos\nMagazine\nApp\nNewsletters\nSweeps\nTV Schedule\nBlog\nFood Network Kitchen App\nShop\nShows A-Z\nChefs A-Z\nLog Out\nLog In\nSign Up\n\u00a9 2020 Television Food Network, G.P. All rights reserved.\nHome\nRecipes\nValerie Bertinelli\nPrev Recipe\nNext Recipe\nWATCH\nWATCH\nLoading Video...\nSee more\n(12)\nChicken and Broccoli Fettuccine Alfredo with Homemade Fettuccine\nRecipe courtesy of Valerie Bertinelli\nRecipe courtesy of Valerie Bertinelli\nShow:\nValerie's Home Cooking\nEpisode:\nBe Prepared!\nChicken and Broccoli Fettuccine Alfredo with Homemade Fettuccine\nGetting reviews...\nSave Recipe\nLevel:\nEasy\nTotal:\n3 hr 40 min\n(includes resting time)\nActive:\n1 hr 25 min\nYield:\n4 to 6 servings\nShare This Recipe\nPinterest\nFacebook\nTwitter\nEmail\nLevel:\nEasy\nTotal:\n3 hr 40 min\n(includes resting time)\nActive:\n1 hr 25 min\nYield:\n4 to 6 servings\nIngredients\nHomemade Fettuccine:\n1 1/2 cups plus 3 tablespoons all-purpose flour (about 8 ounces), plus extra if needed\n1/2 teaspoon kosher salt\u00a0\n3 large eggs\u00a0plus 2 yolks\u00a0\nChicken and Broccoli Alfredo:\n1 pound broccoli florets, large pieces cut in half or quartered\n4 tablespoons extra-virgin olive oil\n2 teaspoons lemon zest (2 lemons)\nKosher salt and freshly ground black pepper\n2 tablespoons unsalted butter\u00a0\n1 1/4 to 1 1/2 pounds boneless, skinless chicken breasts (3 small breasts)\u00a0\n1 tablespoon minced garlic (4 cloves)\u00a0\n3 tablespoons all-purpose flour\u00a0\n4 cups half-and-half\u00a0\n1 cup shredded Asiago cheese\n1 cup shredded Parmesan\u00a0\n2 tablespoons fresh lemon juice (1 lemon)\u00a0\n2 tablespoons chopped fresh parsley\u00a0\nDirections\nWATCH\nWatch how to make this recipe.\nFor the homemade fettuccine: Combine the flour and salt in a stand mixer fitted with the dough hook. Add the eggs and yolks and mix on medium speed. Turn the mixer off and scrape down the sides of the bowl, pushing the flour towards the center. Continue to mix on medium speed, repeating these steps until the dough comes together into a ball. If the dough sticks to the sides of the bowl, add flour, 1 tablespoon at a time, until it forms a cohesive ball. Knead the dough on medium-high for 3 to 4 minutes. When the dough is smooth, bright yellow in color and bounces back when pressed, transfer it to a lightly floured work surface. Knead by hand a few more times and then form into a ball. The dough should feel moist but not sticky; knead in more flour, 1 tablespoon at a time, as necessary. Wrap the dough in plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 2 hours but no more than 4 hours.\nFit the stand mixer with the pasta roller attachment and set to the widest setting (No. 1). Position the stand mixer with 2 to 3 feet of counter space to the left. Remove the dough from the refrigerator and divide into three portions. Work with one piece of dough at time, keeping the rest under plastic wrap so it doesn't dry out.\nWith your fingers, press a portion of the dough into a roughly 5-by-2 1/2-inch rectangle. Dust lightly with flour on both sides. Turn the mixer onto low speed and feed the dough through the roller with the 2 1/2-inch parallel to the roller. Next, fold the two ends of the dough into the center so they just meet and then fold one half over the other so the dough closes like a book; this is called laminating the dough. Use your fingers to seal the two edges together, then once again shape the dough into a 5-by-2 1/2-inch rectangle. Dust the dough with flour and feed it through the roller a second time. Repeat by laminating the dough one more time and feeding it through the roller. Dust with flour and feed through the roller three more times, dust with more flour as needed.\nAdjust the roller to setting No. 3 and feed the dough through the roller twice. Adjust to setting No. 5 and feed the dough through two more times. At this point the dough will be over a foot long. Use your right hand to feed the dough through the roller and your left hand to catch the dough. Always be very gentle with the dough to prevent tearing. Be sure to feed the dough through the machine so that it does not fold onto itself. You can make small adjustments to how the dough is entering the roller by gently guiding it to the left or right. If the dough is too long to handle, simply cut it in half and work with a smaller portion.\nFinally, adjust the roller to setting No. 7 and feed the dough through another two times. After the dough has gone through the roller for the last time, dust it all over with flour and then fold it over itself and hold under a piece of plastic wrap. Repeat these steps with the remaining two pieces of dough.\nReplace the roller attachment with the fettucine cutter attachment. Dust a baking sheet with flour. Cut the rolled dough into 12-inch pieces and feed through the fettucine cutter on low speed. Twist the fettucine into a nest and place on the prepared baking sheet. Cover with plastic wrap while you cut the remaining dough. Lightly dust the tops of the fettucine nests with flour, cover with slightly dampened paper towel and then with plastic wrap. Hold at room temperature for no more than an hour or the pasta will dry out. (Makes 1 pound pasta dough.)\nFor the chicken and broccoli alfredo: Place a baking sheet in the oven and preheat the oven to 450 degrees F.\nMix the broccoli florets with 2 tablespoons of the olive oil, 1 teaspoon of the lemon zest, and salt and pepper to taste. Add the broccoli to the preheated baking sheet and roast until the lightly charred and tender, 18 minutes. Remove from the oven and let cool.\nBring a large pot of water to a boil. Season with salt so that the water tastes like the ocean.\nHeat a 12-inch, high-sided pan over medium heat. Add the butter and the remaining 2 tablespoons olive oil. Sprinkle the chicken breasts with salt and pepper. When the butter is melted, add the chicken and cook until browned and cooked through, 4 to 5 minutes per side. If the chicken has browned on both sides but isn't cooked through yet, remove to a baking sheet and finish in the oven. Let cool and then cut into 1/2-inch pieces.\nTo the same pan, add the minced garlic; cook until fragrant, 1 minute. Add the flour and stir to combine, scraping up the dark bits from the bottom of the pan. Whisk in 1 cup of the half-and-half, making sure the flour is completely combined, without any lumps. Whisk in the remaining 3 cups half-and-half, bring to a boil and cook for 3 to 4 minutes. When the mixture has thickened around the edges, but before your whisk leaves a trail behind it, add the remaining 1 teaspoon lemon zest and the Asiago and Parmesan, and whisk to combine. Turn the heat to low and season with salt and pepper. The sauce should have the consistency of a thick soup. If the sauce thickens too much, add a little of the pasta water to thin it out. Add the chicken and broccoli to the cheese sauce and hold over low heat.\nMeanwhile, cook to the pasta: Separate the strands of pasta on the baking sheet and add them to the boiling water. Cook for 30 seconds, or until the pasta floats to the top. Drain and add to the cheese sauce. Add the lemon juice and toss to combine. Garnish with parsley and serve immediately.\nMy Private Notes\nAdd a Note\nWATCH\nShow:\nValerie's Home Cooking\nEpisode:\nBe Prepared!\nCategories:\nPasta Recipes\nAlfredo\nChicken Recipes\nPoultry\nBroccoli\nMain Dish\nLooking for Something Else?\nQuick & Easy\nMore Chicken Recipes\n5 Ingredients or Less\nHighly Rated\nChicken Fettuccine Alfredo\nChicken Fettuccine Alfredo\nCajun Chicken Alfredo\nBow-Tie Skillet Alfredo\nChicken Broccoli Casserole\nChicken Stir-Fry\nChicken and Broccoli Stir-Fry\nChicken, Broccoli and Cheese Casserole\nGet the Food Network Kitchen App\n\ud83d\udc69\u200d\ud83c\udf73 What's Cooking\nHealthy Dinners \u2014 Fast!\nTop Cauliflower Recipes\n60+ Spring Dinners\nDiscover More Recipes...\nLet's Get Cooking!\nTo sign up, please enable JavaScript.\nSign up for the Recipe of the Day newsletter to receive editor-picked recipes, tips and videos delivered to your inbox daily. Of course there are tons of jarred pasta sauces you can buy, but making alfredo sauce from scratch is actually so easy.\nThis is a great base recipe for all your one-pot pasta needs. Consider the following revisions when you feel like mixing it up.\nIf you're looking for a richer sauce, substitute heavy cream or half and half for the milk\u2014never a bad move.\nBig fan of dark meat? Swap in thighs for breasts ! Just make sure you give them ample cooking time. Thighs take much longer in the pan, and actually cook best with a quick trip to the oven. Our garlic butter baked chicken thighs utilize this technique, and they're BOMB.\nGet experimental with the noodles : fettuccini is a classic, but angel hair or spaghetti would work just fine! Just make sure whatever pasta you choose can be completely submerged in your cooking liquid.\nFeel like you need some veg? Stir in a couple big handfuls of spinach and some halved grape tomatoes after the pasta is cooked.\nIf you're missing crunch, toast up some panko bread crumbs in a skillet with butter and garnish with a handful. This trick works for any pasta, the added texture really takes it over the top.\nMade it?\u00a0Let us know how it went in the comment section below!\nRead More +\nRead Less -\nAdvertisement - Continue Reading Below\nYields: 4\nPrep Time: 0 hours 10 mins\nTotal Time: 0 hours 30 mins\nIngredients\n2 tbsp.\nextra-virgin olive oil\n2\nboneless skinless chicken breasts\nKosher salt\nFreshly ground black pepper\n1 1/2 c.\nwhole milk\n1 1/2 c.\nlow-sodium chicken broth\n2\ncloves garlic, minced\n8 oz.\nfetuccini\n1/2 c.\nheavy cream\n1 c.\nfreshly grated Parmesan\nFreshly chopped parsley, for garnish\u00a0\nDirections\nIn a large skillet over medium-high heat, heat oil. Add chicken and season with salt and pepper. Cook until golden and cooked through, 8 minutes per side. Let rest 10 minutes, then slice.\u00a0\nAdd milk, broth, and garlic to skillet. Season with salt and pepper and bring to a simmer. Add fettuccine, stirring frequently for about 3 minutes. Let cook until al dente, 8 minutes more.\u00a0\nStir in heavy cream and Parmesan until combined. Simmer until sauce thickens.\u00a0\nRemove from heat and stir in sliced chicken. Garnish with parsley.\u00a0\nEthan Calabrese\nLena Abraham\nFood Editor\nLena Abraham is the Food Editor at Delish, where she develops and styles recipes for video and photo, and also stays on top of current food trends.\nAdvertisement - Continue Reading Below\nMore From\nRecipes\n14 Game-Changing Iced Coffee Hacks\n79 Stupid-Easy Desserts That Only Look Impossible\nAdvertisement - Continue Reading Below\nChicken Fried Rice\nChurro Pull-Apart Muffins\n100+ Brilliant Ways to Top A Burger\nHomemade Rugelach\n\"Fried\" Ice Cream\nSpinach Artichoke Orzo\nTortilla Stromboli\nVegetarian Baked Ziti Is Cheesy Perfection\nRecipes\nMeals & Cooking\nHow to Make Crock Pot Chicken and Dumplings\nSuper Easy Chicken Spaghetti Recipe\nThe Best Teriyaki Chicken Recipe\nHow to Make Chicken Tetrazzini\nThe Best Authentic Jerk Chicken Recipe\nHow to Make Shrimp Alfredo\nNewsletter\nAbout Us\nPress Room\nContact Us\nBestProducts\nCommunity Guidelines\nAdvertise With Us\nA Part of Hearst Digital Media\nDelish participates in various affiliate marketing programs, which means we may get paid commissions on editorially chosen products purchased through our links to retailer sites.\n\u00a92020 Hearst Magazine Media, Inc. Noteworthy changes in Italian cuisine happened with the discovery of the New World\u00a0and the introduction of\u00a0potatoes,\u00a0tomatoes,\u00a0bell peppers\u00a0and maize, which are now an integral part of this cuisine.\u00a0 Italian cuisine is known for its regional diversity each with a distinct taste.\u00a0 This cuisine today is probably one of the most popular in the world.\nPrep Time :\n11-15 minutes\nCook time :\n11-15 minutes\nServe :\n4\nLevel Of Cooking :\nModerate\nTaste :\nMild\nIngredients for Spaghetti in Alfredo Truffle Sauce Recipe\nSpaghetti boiled 250 grams\nButton Mushrooms 8-10\nFew shavings of truffle + for garnishing\nExtra-virgin olive oil 1 tablespoon\nCrushed garlic 1 teaspoon\nSalt to taste\nCrushed black peppercorns to taste\nFresh cream 1 cup\nMethod\nStep 1\nSlice button mushrooms.\nStep 2\nHeat olive oil in a non-stick pan, add garlic and saut\u00c3\u00a9 for a minute. Add mushrooms and saut\u00c3\u00a9 till brown.\nStep 3\nAdd boiled spaghetti, salt, 1 tbsp water, peppercorns and fresh cream and mix well.\nStep 4\nAdd truffle shavings and mix well. Cook for a minute.\nStep 5\nTransfer onto a serving plate, garnish with truffle shavings and serve hot.\nNutrition Info\nCalories : 1540 \u00a0Kcal\nCarbohydrates : 34.6 \u00a0gm\nProtein : 197.4 \u00a0gm\nFat : 68 \u00a0gm\nOther : Iron- 8.2mg\nMost Visited Recipes\nVegetable Biryani\nKhaman Dhokla\nChicken Biryani\nPav Bhajee\nGajar Halwa\nRecently Added Recipes\nTandoori Chaat- Sk Khazana\nPineapple Raita\nPeri Peri Makhana- Sk Khazana\nPapeta Par Eeda - SK Khazana\nPeri Peri Crispy Corn- Sk Khazana\nPeri Peri Chicken Pizza- SK Khazana\nLiked this recipes, Rate us :\n\u00ef\u00bb\u00bf\nHealth Recipes\nHealthy Breakfast\nHealthy Snacks\nHealthy Soups\nHealthy Subzis\nVegan\nChef Sanjeev Kapoor is the most celebrated face of Indian cuisine. Classic Chicken Alfredo is a feel good comfort food \u2013 so creamy but light!\nThis post may contain affiliate links. Read my disclosure policy .\nMom learned how to make this \u201cPollo Chicken Fettuccine Alfredo\u201d in culinary school. She made it for us when we were kids and we were crazy about it. Now I make the same alfredo recipe for my family. It\u2019s one of my favorite comfort foods. Watch the video tutorial and learn how to make chicken alfredo.\nChicken Fettuccini Alfredo\nIngredients for Chicken Fettuccine Alfredo:\nWe usually use chicken breast but chicken tenders would work well if that is what you have on hand.\nFettuccini is the pasta of choice here but we\u2019ve been known to swap with angel hair or vermicelli. You can use a variety of pastas. P.S. sometimes we sneak in the full pound of pasta when feeding a crowd.\u00a0\nSubstitute for Half and Half?\nThis recipe calls for half and half, but you can substitute with equal parts of milk and heavy whipping cream. The half and half thickens as it simmers and even more as it rests. If you prefer a creamier or thicker sauce, you can use heavy whipping cream instead.\u00a0\nHow to Make Chicken Alfredo (Video below):\n1. Cook fettuccini in a large pot of salted water (4 qts water with 1 Tbsp salt,) according to package instructions then drain and set aside.\n2. Meanwhile, thinly slice chicken breast into strips and season all over with salt and pepper. In a large, deep skillet , heat 2 Tbsp\u00a0olive oil over medium/high heat and\u00a0saute chicken until light golden and cooked through (5 min). Remove chicken from the pan and cover to keep warm.\n3. In the same pan over medium/high, add 1 Tbsp\u00a0olive oil and 1 Tbsp butter. Add onion and saut\u00e9 3\u00a0minutes until soft. Add sliced mushrooms and saut\u00e9 until soft (5-7 min), stirring\u00a0frequently.\u00a0Add garlic and saut\u00e9 another 30 seconds until fragrant, stirring constantly.\n4. Add half-n-half and simmer over medium/high heat 8-10 min, or until just beginning to thicken. Add chicken back to pan, along with 1/4 cup parsley and season sauce to taste (1/2 to 1 tsp salt and 1/4 tsp pepper).\n5. Add cooked pasta and stir to combine. Heat another minute until warmed through then turn off the heat, cover and let pasta rest 10-15 minutes then stir to combine and serve garnished with more parsley.\nAfter the pasta rests, you will have a creamy but light Alfredo sauce that coats the noodles perfectly.\nCreamy Pasta Recipes to Try Next:\nCreamy Shrimp Pasta \u2013 juicy shrimp in alfredo sauce\nMushroom and Leek Pasta \u2013 this sauce tastes gourmet\nChicken Pasta in Creamy Tomato Sauce \u2013 easy, excellent dinner idea\nChicken Tetrazzini \u2013\u00a0 Creamy and scrumptious pasta casserole\nWatch How to Make Chicken Fettuccini Alfredo:\nSee Natasha make her Mom\u2019s Chicken Alfredo Recipe. We love hanging out with you on our\u00a0 Youtube Channel !\n\u2b07\ufe0f Print Friendly Chicken Fettuccini Alfredo:\nShare the Post:\nShare on Pinterest\nShare on Facebook\nShare on Twitter\nShare on Yummly\nShare via Email\nPrint\nChicken Fettuccine Alfredo\n4.87 from 68 votes\nPrep Time:\n20\nminutes\nCook Time:\n20\nminutes\nTotal Time:\n35\nminutes\nMom's creamy Chicken Fettuccine Alfredo has been a family favorite for years! Classic Chicken Alfredo is a feel good comfort food - so creamy but light!\nAuthor:\nNatasha of NatashasKitchen.com\nSkill Level:\nEasy/Medium\nCost to Make:\n$13-$15\nKeyword:\nChicken Fettuccine Alfredo\nCalories:\n509\nkcal\nServings:\n8\npeople\nIngredients\n2\nlbs\nChicken Breast\n3/4\nlbs\nfettuccine pasta\n(or angel hair or vermicelli pasta)\n1\nlb\nwhite mushrooms\nthickly sliced\n1\nsmall onion\nfinely chopped\n3\ncloves\ngarlic\nminced\n3 1/2\ncups\nhalf and half\n*\n1/4\ncup\nparsley, finely chopped,\nplus more for garnish\n1\ntsp\nsea salt\nor to taste, plus more for pasta water\n1/4\ntsp\nblack pepper\nor to taste\n3\nTbsp\nolive oil\ndivided\n1\nTbsp\nbutter\nUS Customary - Metric\nInstructions\nCook fettuccini in a pot of salted water (4 qts water, 1 Tbsp salt,) according to package instructions then drain and set aside.\nMeanwhile, slice chicken into strips and season all over with salt and pepper. In a large skillet, heat 2 Tbsp olive oil over medium/high heat and saut\u00e9 chicken until lightly golden and cooked through (5 min). Remove chicken from the pan and cover to keep warm.\nIn the same pan over medium/high, heat 1 Tbsp olive oil and 1 Tbsp of butter. Add onion and saut\u00e9 3 min until soft. Add sliced mushrooms and saut\u00e9 until soft (5-7 min), stirring frequently. Add garlic and saut\u00e9 30 seconds, stirring constantly.\nAdd half-n-half and simmer over medium/high heat 8-10 min, or until beginning to thicken. Add chicken back to the pan, add 1/4 cup parsley and season sauce to taste (1/2 to 1 tsp salt and 1/4 tsp pepper).\nAdd cooked pasta and stir to combine. Heat another minute until warmed through then turn off the heat, cover and let rest 10-15 minutes then stir and serve garnished with parsley.\u00a0\nRecipe Notes\n*To substitute half and half, use equal parts of milk and heavy cream. If you prefer a thicker creamier sauce, you can use heavy whipping cream instead.\u00a0\nNutrition Facts\nChicken Fettuccine Alfredo\nAmount Per Serving\nCalories 509\nCalories from Fat 207\n% Daily Value*\nFat 23g 35%\nSaturated Fat 10g 63%\nCholesterol 151mg 50%\nSodium 491mg 21%\nPotassium 876mg 25%\nCarbohydrates 38g 13%\nFiber 2g 8%\nSugar 2g 2%\nProtein 35g 70%\nVitamin A 635IU 13%\nVitamin C 7.3mg 9%\nCalcium 141mg 14%\nIron 1.8mg 10%\n* Percent Daily Values are based on a 2000 calorie diet.\nNutrition Disclosure\nInstagram\nIf you make this recipe, I\u2019d love to see pics of your creations on Instagram, Facebook and Twitter! Noteworthy changes in Italian cuisine happened with the discovery of the New World\u00a0and the introduction of\u00a0potatoes,\u00a0tomatoes,\u00a0bell peppers\u00a0and maize, which are now an integral part of this cuisine.\u00a0 Italian cuisine is known for its regional diversity each with a distinct taste.\u00a0 This cuisine today is probably one of the most popular in the world.\nPrep Time :\n11-15 minutes\nCook time :\n21-25 minutes\nServe :\n4\nLevel Of Cooking :\nModerate\nTaste :\nMild\nIngredients for Macaroni Alfredo Recipe\nMacaroni 1 packet\nMilk 1/4 cup\nParsley a few sprigs\nButter 1 tablespoon\nGarlic 2-3 cloves\nFresh cream 3/4 cup\nSalt to taste\nCream cheese 3 teaspoon\nWhite pepper powder optional to taste\nParmesan cheese grated optional\nMethod\nStep 1\nHeat plenty of water in a deep non stick pan. Keep a sieve over it and put macaroni and salt in it and cook till al dente.\nStep 2\nChop parsley. Heat butter in a non stick pan. Crush garlic and add and saut\u00c3\u00a9 for 1 minute. Add fresh cream and milk and mix well.\nStep 3\nAdd cream cheese and mix well and cook for 1-2 minutes. Add salt and pepper powder if you wish to.\nStep 4\nDrain the macaroni and add to the sauce and mix well.\nStep 5\nAdd parsley and mix. Serve hot.\nStep 6\nIf you wish you can garnish with a little parmesan cheese.\nNutrition Info\nCalories : 1896 \u00a0Kcal\nCarbohydrates : 47 \u00a0gm\nProtein : 300.4 \u00a0gm\nFat : 56.1 \u00a0gm\nOther : 0\nMost Visited Recipes\nVegetable Biryani\nKhaman Dhokla\nChicken Biryani\nPav Bhajee\nGajar Halwa\nRecently Added Recipes\nTandoori Chaat- Sk Khazana\nPineapple Raita\nPeri Peri Makhana- Sk Khazana\nPapeta Par Eeda - SK Khazana\nPeri Peri Crispy Corn- Sk Khazana\nPeri Peri Chicken Pizza- SK Khazana\nLiked this recipes, Rate us :\n\u00ef\u00bb\u00bf\nHealth Recipes\nHealthy Breakfast\nHealthy Snacks\nHealthy Soups\nHealthy Subzis\nVegan\nChef Sanjeev Kapoor is the most celebrated face of Indian cuisine. It\u2019s absolutely decadent, made with a cashew cream sauce, and the sauce is made easily in your blender!\nWhere do I start? You\u2019re going to absolutely love and want to devour this Vegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta. I\u2019m talking cheesy, creamy, absolutely indulgent in taste kind of pasta dinner. The kind of dinner that totally hits the spot, and makes you want to curl up on a Friday night. Without the heavy feeling, of course. All my pasta cravings are hereby conquered.\nFirst things first \u2013 I haven\u2019t been a big pasta fanatic. LET me be clear. When a pasta dish is done well \u2013 I am all for that. If you\u2019re a vegetarian or a vegan though, you know that\u00a0 lots of pasta dishes just are\u00a0 not done correctly. Kind of a leftover, oh yeah whoops, kind of scenario, and it can drive you to never want to have pasta again.\nWHAT a terrible nightmarish scenario. Fortunately, after making this Vegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta, I now know I have the best pasta dish sitting and waiting at home on me! You\u2019re going to want to grab some cashews right now so that you can make this for dinner, friends.\nLet\u2019s talk key ingredients. That roasted garlic is a\u00a0 must . I mean, it deepens the flavour of the entire sauce, and really brings it to another level. You\u2019re going to have to wait for your cashews to soak anyway, so you might as well make it. I guarantee it\u2019ll change all of your dishes.\nSpeaking of which, cashews. OMG. Adding soaked cashews to this sauce makes it so creamy and gives it that traditional white colour. No, the sauce won\u2019t taste like cashews, thanks to the addition of another ingredient: lemon or lime juice. This acid helps to neutralise the cashew flavour so all you taste is the cheesiness.\nThe nutritional yeast and the vegan parmesan cheese! I speak all about nutritional yeast here , and I made a vegan parmesan cheese for you here. You can also buy your vegan parm though, so it\u2019s totally up to you. That extra bit of tanginess really ups the sauce, and you can add eons of it on top too. The nutritional yeast in the Alfredo sauce gives it that cheesy flavour, that will have you taste testing the heck out of this sauce.\nAlmond milk and pasta water! Don\u2019t use regular water! Pasta water already has some saltiness, some starch, and is a perfectly seasoned form of water in this sauce. The almond milk of course adds more creaminess.\nBasically what I\u2019m saying is, friends, every ingredient is key here. Including the cooked down onions (adding a nice flavour + umami). What you get is a beautiful vegan Alfredo sauce recipe made in your blender that you can pour back on your pasta and then dig in. The kind of sauce you\u2019ll probably want to put on anything, but will definitely slather all over your pasta.\nThat\u2019s it! Your pasta dreams have come true! Dive in friends, and enjoy!\n\u00a0\nVegan Garlic Alfredo Pasta\nby: Jessica in the Kitchen\nPrep Time 1\nminute\nCook Time 15\nminutes\nTotal Time 16\nminutes\nCourse Dinner, Lunch\nKeyword Dairy Free, Egg Free, Nut Free, Soy Free, vegan, Vegetarian\nPrint\nShare\nFacebook\nTwitter\nGoogle+\nPinterest\nYummly\nTumblr\nEmail\n5 from 3 votes\nIngredients\nPasta\n12\nounces\nany pasta\nI used fettuccine\nchopped parsley\nfor garnish\nVegan Alfredo Sauce\n2\nteaspoons\nvegan butter or olive oil\n1/2\nred onion\nchopped\n1\ncup\ncashews\nsoaked overnight, or in hot water for one hour\n1/4\ncup\npasta water\n1 \u00bd\ncups\nunsweetened almond milk\n4\ncloves\nroasted garlic*\n2\ntablespoons\nnutritional yeast\n\u00bd\nteaspoon\nsea salt\n2\ntablespoons\nvegan parmesan cheese + extra for topping\n1\ntablespoon\nlime juice\nInstructions\nInstructions\nCook pasta according to package directions in a well salted pot of water. Reserve \u00bc cup of the pasta water.\nWhile the pasta is boiling/you're waiting for the water to boil, in a pan over medium high heat, heat the vegan butter or olive oil. Add the onion, stir and let cook until translucent, about 5 minutes.\nRemove the onions from the pan and add it to a blender. Add the rinsed off soaked cashews (without the water), the pasta water, the almond milk, the roasted garlic, the nutritional yeast, the sea salt the vegan parmesan cheese and the lime juice. Blend it all together until completely creamy. If you have a high powered blender this will happen quickly, about 1 minute, if not, just keep blending until completely smooth and creamy. Taste and add more salt or vegan parmesan cheese if necessary.\nWhen the pasta is finished boiling, drain and pour back into the pan you had used earlier or even into a Tupperware container if you want. Pour the Alfredo sauce over and stir to combine completely.\nWhen serving, top with parsley to garnish and more vegan parmesan cheese. Enjoy!\nVideo\nNOTES\n*YES roasted garlic takes about 40 minutes, but you\u2019ll need to wait for your cashews to soak for an hour at least anyway! Cut a bit of the tops off of a whole head of garlic, put it in foil, drizzle olive oil on it, wrap the foil around it and cook it at 450 degrees F for 45 minutes in your oven until the cloves are soft and velvety! Allow it to cool, then push the cloves out.\n\u00a0\nYou can reheat this! Just reheat it in a stove top over medium high heat with a bit more almond milk to thin it out again until hot.\nPrep time doesn\u2019t include soaking the cashews overnight.\nby Jessica\n_-jbxMmYlqE\nShare This Post\nPost navigation\n\u2039\u2039 Older Posts\nNewer Posts \u203a\u203a\nYou Might Also Like\nChocolate Chia Pudding (5 Ingredients, Vegan, Low Carb)\nRead More\nHow To Make Cashew Cream (The Ultimate Dairy Free Substitute)\nRead More\nEasy Grilled Pineapples (aka Caramelised Pineapples)\nRead More\nleave a comment Cancel reply\nRecipe Rating\n40 comments\nComment navigation\nOlder Comments\nErica\nsays:\nI\u2019m allergic to cashews, what would you suggest?\nDecember 10, 2018\nReply\nJessica\nsays:\nHi Erica,\nMaybe macadamia nuts?
